\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{checkArgumentName()}{checkArgumentName()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Doc\+Parser\+::check\+Argument\+Name (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Collects the parameters found with @param command in a list context.\+params\+Found. If the parameter is not an actual parameter of the current member context.\+member\+Def, then a warning is raised (unless warnings are disabled altogether).

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Doc\+Parser\+::check\+Un\+Or\+Multiple\+Documented\+Params (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Checks if the parameters that have been specified using @param are indeed all parameters and that a parameter does not have multiple @param blocks. Must be called after \mbox{\hyperlink{class_doc_parser_ad426893f12b2bc919bc61b3d95e8f471}{check\+Argument\+Name()}} has been called for each argument.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{findDocsForMemberOrCompound()}{findDocsForMemberOrCompound()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Doc\+Parser\+::find\+Docs\+For\+Member\+Or\+Compound (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_string}{QCString}} \&}]{command\+Name,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_string}{QCString}} $\ast$}]{p\+Doc,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_string}{QCString}} $\ast$}]{p\+Brief,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_definition}{Definition}} $\ast$$\ast$}]{p\+Def }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Looks for a documentation block with name command\+Name in the current context (g\+\_\+parser\+Context.\+context). The resulting documentation string is put in p\+Doc, the definition in which the documentation was found is put in p\+Def. 
\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em TRUE} & if name was found. \\
\hline
{\em FALSE} & if name was not found. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Doc\+Parser\+::handle\+Pending\+Style\+Commands (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2src_2docnode_8h_a50a8832c21dd4d026a4ca85c1efb57ec}{Doc\+Node\+Variant}} $\ast$}]{parent,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_doc_node_list}{Doc\+Node\+List}} \&}]{children }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Called at the end of a paragraph to close all open style changes (e.\+g. a {\bfseries{ without a }}). The closed styles are pushed onto a stack and entered again at the start of a new paragraph.
